[bits 64]
basm_cpuinfo:
push rbx
xor eax, eax; cpuid
mov r8, basm_cpuid_str
mov [r8+0], ebx
mov [r8+4], edx
mov [r8+8], ecx
xor eax, eax; inc eax; cpuid
mov r8, basm_cpuid_std
mov [r8+0], eax
mov [r8+4], ebx
mov [r8+8], ecx
mov [r8+12], edx
pop rbx; ret
basm_getbp: mov rax, rbp; ret
